				}			
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = slothful
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Sorry for disturbing
		name = VIETmisc.8132.a
		piety = 1
		random_list = {
			15 = { add_trait = humble }
			15 = { add_trait = kind }
			15 = { add_trait = brave }
			55 = { }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = craven
			}
			remove_trait = craven
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			long_character_event = { id = VIETmisc.8134 }
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Quietly gtfo
		name = VIETmisc.8132.b
		random_list = {
			50 = { piety = 1 }
			50 = { prestige = 1 }
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Not scared
		name = VIETmisc.8132.c
		prestige = 1
		add_trait = brave
		add_trait = proud
		hidden_tooltip = {
			long_character_event = { id = VIETmisc.8133 }
		}
	}
}

character_event = {

	desc = VIETmisc.8136.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_ancient_cairn
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		#NOT = { religion_group = pagan_group }
		capital_scope = {
			OR = {
				region = world_europe_west
				region = world_europe_south
				region = world_asia_minor
				region = world_persia
				region = world_africa_north
				region = world_middle_east
				region = world_india_rajastan
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_artifact = VIET_hellenic_statue_male }
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.3
			any_artifact = {
				count = 3
				has_artifact_flag = VIET_clutter_flag
			}
		}				
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.3
			any_artifact = {
				has_artifact_flag = VIET_clutter_flag
			}
		}

			factor = 1.2

			factor = 0.8

		}

			factor = 1.2
			trait = diligent
		}

			factor = 0.8
			trait = slothful
		}

			factor = 1.2
			trait = greedy
		}

			factor = 0.8
			trait = charitable
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8

		}

		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8136.a #Bedchamber

			NOR = {
				trait = celibate

				trait = chaste
				AND = {
					is_female = yes
					trait = homosexual
				}
				AND = {
					is_female = no
					NOT = { trait = homosexual }
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				trait = hedonist
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				trait = zealous
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				trait = arbitrary
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				trait = just
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				trait = cruel
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				trait = kind
			}
		}
		piety = -5
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = lustful_ruler
			duration = 365
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = lustful }
			}
			random = {
				add_trait = lustful
				chance = 50
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = muslim
			}
			decadence = 1
		}
		add_artifact = VIET_hellenic_statue_male
		new_artifact = {
			set_creation_date = 1.1.1
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8136.b #DESTROY
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				religion_group = christian
				religion_group = muslim
				religion_group = jewish_group
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				trait = zealous
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				trait = cynical
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				trait = proud
			}
		}
		piety = 5
		if = {

			}
			remove_trait = cynical

			chance = 33

	}
	option = {

			}

			}

# Convert mountainous ancient ruins into something?
province_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8140
	desc = VIETmisc.8140.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_ancient_cairn_swiss
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = VIET_province_converted_mountain_ruins_temple }
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = VIET_province_converted_mountain_ruins_inn }
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = VIET_province_converted_mountain_ruins_outpost }
		terrain = mountain
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 12500
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			owner = {
				OR = {
					is_tribal = yes
					is_nomadic = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			NOT = { num_of_max_settlements = 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			NOT = { num_of_max_settlements = 3 }
		}
	}
	

	option = { # no
		name = VIETmisc.8140.a
	}
	option = { # build shrine with inn
		name = VIETmisc.8140.b
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				OR = {
					wealth = 50
					ai = no				
				}
			}
		}
		owner = {
			wealth = -50
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = VIET_province_converted_mountain_ruins_temple
			duration = 5475
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Reapers"
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = increase_prosperity_custom_tooltip
				hidden_tooltip = {					
					change_variable = { which = prosperity_value value = 4 }
				}
			}
		}
	}	
	option = { # build large inn
		name = VIETmisc.8140.c
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				OR = {
					wealth = 50
					ai = no				
				}
			}
		}
		owner = {
			wealth = -50
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = VIET_province_converted_mountain_ruins_inn
			duration = 5475
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Reapers"
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = increase_prosperity_custom_tooltip
				hidden_tooltip = {					
					change_variable = { which = prosperity_value value = 4 }
				}
			}
		}
	}	
	option = { # build outpost with inn
		name = VIETmisc.8140.d
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				OR = {
					wealth = 50
					ai = no				
				}
			}
		}
		owner = {
			wealth = -50
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = VIET_province_converted_mountain_ruins_outpost
			duration = 5475
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Reapers"
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = increase_prosperity_custom_tooltip
				hidden_tooltip = {					
					change_variable = { which = prosperity_value value = 4 }
				}
			}
		}
	}	
}

# Narri - barmaid flirts with character
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8144
	desc = VIETmisc.8144.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_brothel
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no
	only_men = yes
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		has_unattractive_trait_trigger = no
		has_game_rule = {
			name = VIET_events_rules
			value = silly
		}
		#NOT = {
		#	has_game_rule = {
		#		name = VIET_events_rules
		#		value = serious
		#	}
		#}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1	
		modifier = {
			factor = 2			
			has_attractive_trait_trigger = yes
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5			
			has_attractive_trait_trigger = no
		}	
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = greedy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = charitable
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8144.a # Ignore
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = trusting
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = trusting
				chance = 40
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			75 = { }
			15 = { add_trait = cynical }
			5 = { add_trait = paranoid }
			5 = { add_trait = shy }
		}
	}	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8144.b # Friendly chat
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = shy
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = shy
				chance = 30
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				add_trait = gregarious
				chance = 30
			}
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_interesting_talk_with_stranger
			duration = 210
		}
	}	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8144.c # Flirt
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				trait = celibate
				trait = eunuch
				trait = homosexual
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = chaste
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = chaste
				chance = 25
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = shy
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = shy
				chance = 70
			}
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = lustful_ruler
			duration = 210
		}
	}	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8144.d # Bang
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				trait = celibate
				trait = eunuch
				trait = homosexual
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = chaste
			}
			remove_trait = chaste
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				add_trait = lustful
				chance = 75
			}
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_one_time_lovemaking
			duration = 365
		}
	}	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8144.e # Not into women
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				trait = celibate
				trait = eunuch
				trait = homosexual
			}
		}
		piety = 5
	}
}

# It's a fine day with you around - character meets young noble
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8145
	desc = VIETmisc.8145.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_dancing
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		has_game_rule = {
			name = VIET_events_rules
			value = silly
		}
		#NOT = {
		#	has_game_rule = {
		#		name = VIET_events_rules
		#		value = serious
		#	}
		#}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1	
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = charitable
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = greedy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8145.a # Advice and kind words
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = envious
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = envious
				chance = 30
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				add_trait = kind
				chance = 30
			}
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = advice_giver
			duration = 456
		}
	}	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8145.b # Talk to someone else
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = patient
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = patient
				chance = 30
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				add_trait = proud
				chance = 30
			}
		}
	}	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8145.c # Bring to court
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_fine_day_with_you_around }
		}
		set_character_flag = VIET_fine_day_with_you_around
		random_list = {
			70 = { }
			10 = { add_trait = charitable }
			10 = { add_trait = kind }
			10 = { add_trait = humble }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_female = yes
			}
			create_character = {
				age = 18
				dynasty = actually_culture
				religion = ROOT
				culture = ROOT
				female = no
				random_traits = no
				historical = yes
			}
			new_character = {
				#Education & other basic stuff
				#set_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_concubinage
				#set_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_marriage
				set_character_flag = no_court_invites
				random_list = {
					70 = { add_trait = charismatic_negotiator }
					30 = { add_trait = grey_eminence }
				}					
				random = {
					VIET_give_clutter_artifact_effect = yes
					chance = 10
				}	
				#Guaranteed Traits
				add_trait = kind
				add_trait = humble
				add_trait = shy
				add_trait = trusting
				add_trait = fair
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_loyal_servant
					who = ROOT
					years = 100
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_female = no
			}
			create_character = {
				age = 18
				dynasty = actually_culture
				religion = ROOT
				culture = ROOT
				female = yes
				random_traits = no
				historical = yes
			}
			new_character = {
				#Education & other basic stuff
				#set_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_concubinage
				#set_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_marriage
				set_character_flag = no_court_invites
				random_list = {
					70 = { add_trait = charismatic_negotiator }
					30 = { add_trait = grey_eminence }
				}					
				random = {
					VIET_give_clutter_artifact_effect = yes
					chance = 10
				}	
				#Guaranteed Traits
				add_trait = kind
				add_trait = humble
				add_trait = shy
				add_trait = trusting
				add_trait = fair
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_loyal_servant
					who = ROOT
					years = 100
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_nice_day_with_you_around_tooltip }
	}
}


# Jenassa - strange female mercenary comes to court
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8146
	desc = VIETmisc.8146.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_campfire_hf
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_jenassa_event }
		#has_game_rule = {
		#	name = VIET_events_rules
		#	value = silly
		#}
		NOT = {
			has_game_rule = {
				name = VIET_events_rules
				value = serious
			}
		}
		prestige = 200
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1	
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			prestige = 1000
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			NOT = { prestige = 500 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = craven
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = stubborn
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = erudite
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = wroth
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = VIET_jenassa_event
	}
	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8146.a # Hire her
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				ai = no
				wealth = 30
			}
		}
		wealth = -30
		prestige = -30
		create_random_soldier = {
			age = 30
			dynasty = culture
			religion = ROOT
			culture = random
			female = yes
			random_traits = no
			historical = yes
			attributes = {
				diplomacy = 4
				martial = 7
				stewardship = 3
				intrigue = 6
				learning = 4
			}
		}
		new_character = {
			#Education & other basic stuff
			set_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_concubinage
			set_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_marriage
			set_character_flag = no_court_invites
			set_character_flag = special_marshal
			#Guaranteed Traits
			add_trait = brave
			add_trait = cynical
			add_trait = patient
			add_trait = deceitful
			add_trait = erudite
			add_trait = adventurer
			add_trait = schemer
			add_artifact = bow_tier_2_new
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_loyal_servant
				who = ROOT
				years = 100
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_jenassa_mercenary
				duration = -1
			}
			#Flavor
			random_list = {
				90 = { add_scarred_tiered_effect = yes }
				10 = { 
					trigger = { has_dlc = Reapers }
					add_trait = one_eyed
				}
			}
			random = {
				add_trait = fair
				chance = 25
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8146.b # Don't hire
	}
	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8146.c # Be sexist
		trigger = {
			is_female = no
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_sexist_against_women
			duration = 900
		}
	}
}

		}

			5 = { add_trait = diligent }

			5 = { add_trait = zealous }

			80 = { }

			5 = { add_trait = proud }

	option = {

		piety = 1

			add_trait = humble
			add_trait = gregarious
			add_trait = chaste
			add_trait = just

				VIET_give_generic_weapon_effect = yes
				chance = 20
			}	
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_loyal_servant
				who = ROOT
				years = 100
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_jon_battle_born_soldier
				duration = -1
			}
			#Flavor
			random_list = {
				20 = { add_scarred_tiered_effect = yes }
				80 = { 	}
			}
			random = {
				add_trait = fair
				chance = 20
			}
			random = {
				add_trait = strong
				chance = 35
			}
		}		
	}

# Lydia - A maid is sworn to carry your burdens
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8152
	desc = VIETmisc.8152.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_castle_construction
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		has_game_rule = {
			name = VIET_events_rules
			value = silly
		}
		#NOT = {
		#	has_game_rule = {
		#		name = VIET_events_rules
		#		value = serious
		#	}
		#}
		NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_lydia_maid }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1	

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = cruel
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			lower_tier_than = DUKE
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = stubborn
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = VIET_lydia_maid
	}
	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8152.a # Bad
		prestige = 1
		random_list = {
			70 = { }
			10 = { add_trait = wroth }
			10 = { add_trait = proud }
			10 = { add_trait = stubborn }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8152.b # Good
		piety = 1
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = highly_amused_ruler
			duration = 365
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8152.c # Bring to court
		prestige = -10
		create_character = {
			age = 22
			dynasty = none
			religion = ROOT
			culture = ROOT
			female = yes
			health = 5.5
			random_traits = no
			historical = yes
			attributes = {
				diplomacy = 4
				martial = 6
				stewardship = 4
				intrigue = 4
				learning = 4
			}
		}
		new_character = {
			#Education & other basic stuff
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_lydia_modifier
				duration = -1
			}
			set_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_concubinage
			set_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_marriage
			set_character_flag = VIET_lydia_character
			reverse_opinion = { 
				who = ROOT
				modifier = VIET_opinion_sarcastic_lydia
				years = 100
			}
			set_character_flag = no_court_invites
			random_list = {
				10 = { add_random_education_trait = intrigue }
				10 = { add_random_education_trait = martial }
				10 = { add_random_education_trait = stewardship }
			}					
			random = {
				VIET_give_clutter_artifact_effect = yes
				chance = 10
			}		
			#Guaranteed Traits
			add_trait = robust
			add_trait = cynical
			add_trait = honest
			add_trait = diligent
			add_trait = brave
			add_trait = humble
			random = {
				add_trait = fair
				chance = 20
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_loyal_servant
				who = ROOT
				years = 100
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_why_hire_lydia }
	}
}


# Mithorpa Nasyal (unused NPC) - come across a peasant who initially lashes out but apologises
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8153
	desc = VIETmisc.8153.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_tuscan_country
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		#has_game_rule = {
		#	name = VIET_events_rules
		#	value = silly
		#}
		#NOT = {
		#	has_game_rule = {
		#		name = VIET_events_rules
		#		value = serious
		#	}
		#}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1	

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = craven
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = arbitrary
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8153.a # Forgive him
		trigger = {
			NOT = { trait = cruel }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = wroth
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = wroth
				chance = 55
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = proud
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = proud
				chance = 30
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			70 = { }
			15 = { add_trait = patient }
			15 = { add_trait = humble }
		}
		prestige = -4
		piety = 2
	}
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8153.b # I was trying to be friendly!
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = patient
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = patient
				chance = 55
			}
		}
		prestige = -2
	}
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8153.c # Tell guards to teach him a lesson
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = kind
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = kind
				chance = 55
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			70 = { }
			20 = { add_trait = wroth }
			10 = { add_trait = proud }
		}
		piety = -2
	}
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8153.d # Tell guards to imprison him
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				trait = kind
				trait = just
				trait = patient
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			60 = { }
			20 = { add_trait = wroth }
			10 = { add_trait = cruel }
			10 = { add_trait = arbitrary }
		}
		piety = -4
	}
}


# Sinmir - Elderly townsman criticizes your security
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8154
	desc = VIETmisc.8154.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_village_at_night
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		#has_game_rule = {
		#	name = VIET_events_rules
		#	value = silly
		#}
		NOT = {
			has_game_rule = {
				name = VIET_events_rules
				value = serious
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1	

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = honest
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8154.a # Ignore
		prestige = -2
	}	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8154.b # Apologize
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				trait = proud
				trait = wroth
			}
		}
		prestige = -4
		random_list = {
			70 = { }
			10 = { add_trait = humble }
			20 = { add_trait = trusting }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8154.c # Discuss
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = wroth
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = wroth
				chance = 40
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				add_trait = patient
				chance = 25			
			}
		}
		prestige = -4
	}
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8154.d # Tell him to mind his business
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = patient
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = patient
				chance = 25
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			20 = { add_trait = proud }
			10 = { add_trait = cynical }
			70 = { }
		}
		piety = -3
	}
}

# Telrav - encounter a robbed "merchant" on the road - part 2
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8156
	desc = VIETmisc.8156.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_skyrim_forest
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8156.a # Escape
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_telrav_smart }
			NOR = {
				martial = 12
				combat_rating = 15
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			60 = { }
			35 = {
				add_trait = wounded
			}
			5 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					can_be_maimed_trigger = no
				}
				add_maimed_trait_effect = yes
			}
		}
		prestige = -10
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_telrav_fight_a }
	}
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8156.b # Fight back
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_telrav_smart }
			OR = {
				martial = 12
				combat_rating = 15
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			75 = { }
			20 = {
				add_trait = wounded
			}
			5 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					can_be_maimed_trigger = no
				}
				add_maimed_trait_effect = yes
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			40 = { wealth = 10 }
			30 = { wealth = 15 }
			20 = { wealth = 20 }
			10 = { wealth = 25 }
		}
		prestige = 10
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_telrav_fight_b }
	}
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8156.c # Prepared
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = VIET_telrav_smart
		}
		random_list = {
			95 = { }
			4 = {
				add_trait = wounded
			}
			1 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					can_be_maimed_trigger = no
				}
				add_maimed_trait_effect = yes
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			40 = { wealth = 10 }
			30 = { wealth = 15 }
			20 = { wealth = 20 }
			10 = { wealth = 25 }
		}
		prestige = 20
		clr_character_flag = VIET_telrav_smart
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_telrav_fight_c }
	}
}

	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

		in_command = no
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1	

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = chaste
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8157.a # Buy some
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				ai = no
				wealth = 10
			}
		}
		wealth = -10
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_trader_joes_21_seasoning_salute
			duration = 730
		}
	}	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8157.b # Buy a lot
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				ai = no
				wealth = 25
			}
		}
		wealth = -25
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_trader_joes_21_seasoning_salute
			duration = 1825
		}
	}	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8157.c # No need
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = gluttonous
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = gluttonous
				chance = 30
			}
		}
	}
}

# In eastern religions, garlic and onion makes you horny - cut down on it?
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8159
	desc = VIETmisc.8159.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_VIET_food
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	religion_group = indian_group
	
	trigger = {
	#	in_command = no	
		NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1	

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = paranoid
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8159.a # Won't give up on food
		piety = -3
		prestige = 3
	}	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8159.b # Eat less
		piety = 3
		prestige = -3
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = gluttonous
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = gluttonous
				chance = 15
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				add_trait = temperate
				chance = 15
			}
		}
	}	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8159.c # Want to stimulate self?
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				trait = chaste
				trait = celibate
				trait = eunuch
			}
		}
		piety = -3
		random_list = {
			80 = {
				add_character_modifier = {
					name = lustful_ruler
					duration = 365
				}			
			}
			20 = {
				add_trait = lustful
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8159.d # Silly fear of a plant!
		trigger = {
			NOT = { trait = zealous }
		}
		piety = -3
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = trusting
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = trusting
				chance = 20
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				add_trait = cynical
				chance = 25
			}
		}
	}
}

# Courtier comes to a mosque after eating garlic
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8160
	desc = VIETmisc.8160.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_bishop_muslim
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	religion_group = muslim
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		any_courtier = {
			is_adult = yes
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			ai = yes
			OR = {
				trait = gluttonous
				trait = cynical
				trait = slothful
				trait = proud
				trait = stubborn
				trait = deceitful
			}
			NOT = { trait = zealous }
			NOT = { trait = temperate }
		}
		NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1	

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = trusting
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_adult = yes
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				ai = yes
				OR = {
					trait = gluttonous
					trait = cynical
					trait = slothful
					trait = proud
					trait = stubborn
					trait = deceitful
				}
				NOT = { trait = zealous }
				NOT = { trait = temperate }
			}
			save_event_target_as = target_VIET_muslim_garlic_courtier
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8160.a # Don't do anything
		piety = -5
		random_list = {
			80 = { }
			10 = { add_trait = slothful }
			10 = { add_trait = content }
		}
		random = {
			decadence = 1
			chance = 50
		}
		event_target:target_VIET_muslim_garlic_courtier = {
			piety = -5
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8160.b # Tell courtier it isn't acceptable
		piety = 5
		random = {
			decadence = -1
			chance = 25
		}
		event_target:target_VIET_muslim_garlic_courtier = {
			piety = -5
			opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_calmly_corrected_error
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_garlic_breath
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8160.c # Tell courtier to leave
		piety = 5
		random = {
			decadence = -1
			chance = 25
		}
		event_target:target_VIET_muslim_garlic_courtier = {
			piety = -5
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_sad
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_garlic_breath
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8160.d # Publically shame courtier
		prestige = 5
		random = {
			decadence = -1
			chance = 50
		}
		random = {
			add_trait = zealous
			chance = 25
		}
		event_target:target_VIET_muslim_garlic_courtier = {
			piety = -5
			prestige = -5
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_angry
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_garlic_breath
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

# Bathe in saffron to cure depression/stress?
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8165
	desc = VIETmisc.8165.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_bad_news
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		OR = {
			culture_group = iranian
			culture_group = serindian # exists in WtWSMS
			culture_group = arabic
			culture_group = byzantine
			culture_group = indo_aryan_group
			culture_group = dravidian_group
			capital_scope = {
				region = world_steppe_tarim
				region = world_persia
				region = world_middle_east
				region = world_india
				region = world_africa_north
				region = world_europe_south
				region = world_asia_minor
			}
		}
		OR = {
			trait = depressed
			trait = stressed
		}
		wealth = 20
		NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1	

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = envious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = kind
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8165.a # Use
		wealth = -20
		piety = 5
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = depressed
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = depressed
				chance = 50
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = stressed
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = stressed
				chance = 50
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = muslim
			}
			random = {
				decadence = 1
				chance = 25
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8165.b # Don't use		
	}
	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8165.c # Doesn't work
		if = {
			limit = { 
				trait = trusting
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = trusting
				chance = 33
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				add_trait = cynical
				chance = 25
			}		
		}
	}
}

# Bathe in saffron as an aphrodasiac?
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8166
	desc = VIETmisc.8166.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_lovers
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		OR = {
			culture_group = iranian
			culture_group = serindian # exists in WtWSMS
			culture_group = arabic
			culture_group = byzantine
			culture_group = indo_aryan_group
			culture_group = dravidian_group
			capital_scope = {
				OR = {
					region = world_steppe_tarim
					region = world_persia
					region = world_middle_east
					region = world_india
					region = world_africa_north
					region = world_europe_south
					region = world_asia_minor				
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = { trait = eunuch }
		NOT = { trait = celibate }
		wealth = 20
		NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1	

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = patient
		}

			factor = 0.8
			trait = wroth
		}

			factor = 1.2
			has_lover = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			is_married = yes
			trait = chaste
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8166.a # Use with spouse
		trigger = {
			is_married = yes

				NOT = { trait = celibate }
				NOT = { trait = eunuch }
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
			}
		}
		wealth = -20
		random_spouse = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = celibate }
				NOT = { trait = eunuch }
				NOT = { trait = incapable }			
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_romantic_saffron_bath
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_romantic_saffron_bath
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_saffron_bath
				duration = 365
			}
			random = {
				add_lover = ROOT
				chance = 25
			}
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_saffron_bath
			duration = 365
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = muslim
			}
			decadence = 1
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8166.b # Use with lover

# Courtier offers caraway breath freshener for everyone
character_event = {

	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		any_courtier = {
			#count = 3
			is_adult = yes
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1	

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = envious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = deceitful
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_adult = yes
				NOT = { trait = incapable }			
			}
			save_event_target_as = target_VIET_caraway_courtier
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8172.a # Ok
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_caraway_breath_freshener
			duration = 145
		}
		event_target:target_VIET_caraway_courtier = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_happy
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_happy
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_caraway_breath_freshener
				duration = 145
			}		
		}
	}	
	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8172.b # Ok
		event_target:target_VIET_caraway_courtier = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_caraway_breath_freshener
				duration = 145
			}		
		}
	}	
	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8172.c # Ok
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = trusting
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = trusting
				chance = 55
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				add_trait = paranoid
				chance = 40
			}
		}
		event_target:target_VIET_caraway_courtier = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_suspicious
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_lack_of_trust
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_caraway_breath_freshener
				duration = 145
			}		
		}
	}	
}

			factor = 1.2

			factor = 1.2
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8

		}
		modifier = {

		}

		}

		}

	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no

		in_command = no
		OR = {
			culture = frisian

		}
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1	

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = cruel
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = arbitrary
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8178.a # Eat it all
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = eating_good_food
			duration = 365
		}
		any_courtier = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = eating_good_food
				duration = 365
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8178.b # Pay the farmer
		wealth = -7
		random = {
			add_trait = charitable
			chance = 30
		}

			duration = 365
		}

			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = eating_good_food
				duration = 365
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8178.c # Give it to the poor
		wealth = -7
		piety = 10
		random = {
			add_trait = charitable
			chance = 60
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8178.d # Don't like this!

			60 = { }

			10 = { add_trait = temperate }

			10 = { add_trait = cynical }
		}
	}

# Stupid courtier thinks the grains of paradise actually came from heaven
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8181
	desc = VIETmisc.8181.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_feast_hf
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		any_courtier = {
			is_adult = yes
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			OR = {
				is_dumb_trigger = yes
				trait = trusting
			}
		}
		OR = {
			culture_group = iberian
			culture_group = latin
			culture_group = west_germanic
			culture_group = central_germanic
			culture_group = north_germanic
			culture_group = byzantine
			culture_group = south_slavic
			culture_group = east_slavic
			culture_group = west_slavic
			culture_group = baltic
			culture_group = finno_ugric
		}
		capital_scope = {
			region = world_europe
		}
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1	

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = deceitful
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {

		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_adult = yes
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				OR = {
					is_dumb_trigger = yes
					trait = trusting
				}
			}
			save_event_target_as = target_VIET_grains_of_paradise_dumb
		}
		
	}
	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8181.a # Ok
		event_target:target_VIET_grains_of_paradise_dumb = {
			prestige = -5
		}		
	}	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8181.b # Ok
		event_target:target_VIET_grains_of_paradise_dumb = {
			prestige = -5
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_comforted_me
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
		}
		prestige = -5
		random_list = {
			70 = { }
			10 = { add_trait = kind }
			10 = { add_trait = humble }
			10 = { add_trait = patient }
		}
	}		
	option = { # Name drop Pliny
		name = VIETmisc.8181.c
		tooltip_info = scholar
		trigger = {
			trait = scholar
		}
		prestige = 5
		event_target:target_VIET_grains_of_paradise_dumb = {
			prestige = -5
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_comforted_me
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
		}
	}		
	option = { # Name drop Pliny
		name = VIETmisc.8181.c
		tooltip_info = learning
		trigger = {
			learning = 11
			NOT = { trait = scholar }
		}
		prestige = 5	
		event_target:target_VIET_grains_of_paradise_dumb = {
			prestige = -5
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_comforted_me
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

# Heartbroken servant can't afford herbal concoction to heal wounded heart (gender not specified)
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8185
	desc = VIETmisc.8185.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1	

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = envious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = charitable
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = greedy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = wroth
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8185.a # Help them
		wealth = -10
		piety = 4
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = cruel
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = cruel
				chance = 40
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = greedy
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = greedy
				chance = 30
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = cynical
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = cynical
				chance = 20
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			60 = { }
			15 = { add_trait = kind }
			15 = { add_trait = charitable }
			10 = { add_trait = humble }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = muslim
			}
			random = {
				decadence = -1
				chance = 33
			}
		}
	}	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8185.b # Don't help them
	}	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8185.c # Inspire them
		trigger = {
			diplomacy = 11
		}
		tooltip_info = diplomacy
		prestige = 4
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = cruel
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = cruel
				chance = 30
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				add_trait = kind
				chance = 40
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = muslim
			}
			random = {
				decadence = -1
				chance = 66
			}
		}		
	}
}

# Herbalists become famous
province_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8191
	desc = VIETmisc.8191.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_court_physician
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = VIET_province_famous_herbalists }
		owner = {
			is_nomadic = no
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 7500
	}
	

	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.8191.a
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = VIET_province_famous_herbalists
			duration = 10950
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Reapers"
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = increase_prosperity_custom_tooltip
				hidden_tooltip = {					
					change_variable = { which = prosperity_value value = 4 }
				}
			}
		}
	}	
}

# Courtier is growing an impressive rose garden
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8196
	desc = VIETmisc.8196.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_garden
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
		NOR = {
			is_tribal = yes
			is_nomadic = yes
		}
		capital_scope = {
			NOR = {
				region = world_africa_west
				region = world_africa_east
				region = world_africa_central
				region = world_steppe
				terrain = desert
				terrain = arctic
			}
		}
		any_courtier = {
			is_adult = yes
			ai = yes
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			NOT = { is_consort = ROOT }
			NOT = { is_close_relative = ROOT }
			OR = {
				trait = gardener
				trait = diligent
				trait = patient
				trait = shy
				trait = content
				trait = deceitful
				stewardship = 8
				intrigue = 8
			}
			NOT = { trait = wroth }
			NOT = { trait = slothful }
			NOT = { trait = ambitious }
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1	
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = craven
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_adult = yes
				ai = yes
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				NOT = { is_consort = ROOT }
				NOT = { is_close_relative = ROOT }
				OR = {
					trait = gardener
					trait = diligent
					trait = patient
					trait = shy
					trait = content
					trait = deceitful
					stewardship = 8
					intrigue = 8
				}
				NOT = { trait = wroth }
				NOT = { trait = slothful }
				NOT = { trait = ambitious }			
			}
			save_event_target_as = target_VIET_rose_garden_courtier
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8196.a # Help me with gardening
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_garden_improvements
			duration = 1000
		}
		event_target:target_VIET_rose_garden_courtier = {
			add_trait = gardener
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_rose_garden
				duration = -1
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_asked_me_for_garden_advice
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_garden_advice
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}		
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8196.b # Praise
		event_target:target_VIET_rose_garden_courtier = {
			add_trait = gardener
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_rose_garden
				duration = -1
			}
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_praised_me
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}		
		}
	}	
	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8196.c # Anyone could've done that
		random = {
			add_trait = cynical
			chance = 50
		}
		event_target:target_VIET_rose_garden_courtier = {
			add_trait = gardener
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_rose_garden
				duration = -1
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_gardening_discussions
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}	
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_gardening_discussions
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}		
		}
	}		
	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8196.d # Discuss gardening
		trigger = {
			trait = gardener
		}
		tooltip_info = gardener
		event_target:target_VIET_rose_garden_courtier = {
			add_trait = gardener
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_rose_garden
				duration = -1
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_gardening_discussions
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}	
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_gardening_discussions
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}	
			random = {
				add_friend = ROOT
				chance = 50
			}
		}
	}	
}

	}

		}

			factor = 1.2

		}

	}

		}

		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_feeling_jaded_about_life
			duration = 365
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8200.d # Pay for wedding - charitable option

			trait = charitable

		}
		tooltip_info = charitable

		#			NOT = { trait = incapable }
		#			NOT = { is_close_relative = liege }
		#			is_married = no

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes

		in_command = no
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1	
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = proud
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8203.a # ok
		piety = 3
	}
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8203.b # Be polite
		prestige = 3
		random = {
			add_trait = deceitful
			chance = 10
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8203.c # ask about other theological matters
		random = {
			change_learning = 1
			chance = 10
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8203.d # Ask for gardening tips
		trigger = {
			trait = gardener
		}
		tooltip_info = gardener
		random = {
			change_stewardship = 1
			chance = 50
		}
		random = {
			change_learning = 1
			chance = 50
		}
	}

# Buy some musk deer products?
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8206
	desc = VIETmisc.8206.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_market
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		wealth = 20
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1	
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.4
			capital_scope = {
				NOR = {
					region = world_india
					region = world_steppe
					region = world_himalayas
					region = world_persia
					region = world_middle_east
					region = world_africa_east
					region = world_africa_north
					region = world_asia_minor
					region = world_europe_south_east
				}			
			}
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = groomed
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = uncouth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = content
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8206.a # Buy perfumes
		wealth = -30
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_musk_deer_perfume
			duration = 730
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8206.b # Buy soaps
		wealth = -30
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_musk_deer_soap
			duration = 730
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8206.c # Buy medicines
		wealth = -30
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_musk_deer_medicine
			duration = 730
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8206.d # Don't buy any
		piety = 5
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = proud
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = proud
				chance = 50
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = content }
			}
			random = {
				add_trait = content
				chance = 30
			}
		}
	}
}

		}

		add_province_modifier = {
			name = VIET_province_musk_deer

		}
	}

			OR = {

				region = world_india_rajastan
				region = world_steppe_east
				region = world_steppe_tarim
				region = world_himalayas
			}
			OR = {
				terrain = hills
				terrain = mountain
				terrain = steppe
			}		
		}
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1	
				
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = greedy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = charitable
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = cruel
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = kind
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8208.a # Let them go
		trigger = {
			NOT = { trait = just }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = arbitrary }
			}
			random = {
				add_trait = arbitrary
				chance = 30
			}
		}
		prestige = -10
	}
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8208.b # Rid their goods
		prestige = 5
	}
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.8208.c # Take their goods
		random_list = {
			20 = { add_trait = arbitrary }
			20 = { add_trait = greedy }
			60 = { }
		}
		prestige = -10
		piety = -10
		wealth = 25
	}
}

# Man worries about not having enough experience
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8209
	desc = VIETmisc.8209.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_bad_news
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 13
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	only_men = yes
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		is_virgin_trigger = yes
		NOT = { trait = homosexual }
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1	
				
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = greedy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = stubborn
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = slothful
		}
	}

	option = { #Visit a brothel
		name = VIETmisc.8209.a
		wealth = -5
		piety = -10
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_one_time_lovemaking
			duration = 365
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = chaste
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = chaste
				chance = 75
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = shy
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = shy
				chance = 40
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			70 = { }
			20 = { add_trait = lustful }
			20 = { add_trait = gregarious }
		}
	}
	option = { #Boink a maid
		name = VIETmisc.8209.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = chaste
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = chaste
				chance = 50
			}
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_one_time_lovemaking
			duration = 365
		}
	}
	option = { #Don't care
		name = VIETmisc.8209.c
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_not_enough_sex_rumors
			duration = 365
		}
		random_list = {
			50 = { }
			10 = { add_trait = content }
			10 = { add_trait = slothful }
			30 = { add_trait = chaste }
		}
	}
	option = { #Doesn't like women
		name = VIETmisc.8209.d
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_sexist_against_women
			duration = 365
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_not_enough_sex_rumors
			duration = 365
		}
	}
}

# Young noblewoman loses virtue to rakish scoundrel
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8210
	desc = VIETmisc.8210.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_maiden
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		#is_virgin_trigger = yes
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
		NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_dishonored_maiden_event_already }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1	
				
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = erudite
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = stubborn
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = cruel
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = VIET_dishonored_maiden_event_already 
	}

	option = { #Don't get involved
		name = VIETmisc.8210.a
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_dishonored_maiden_ignore }
	}
	option = { #Look down on girl
		name = VIETmisc.8210.b
		prestige = 5
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_sexist_against_women
			duration = 365
		}
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_dishonored_maiden_scorn }
	}
	option = { #Force man to pay fine
		name = VIETmisc.8210.c
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = arbitrary
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = arbitrary
				chance = 55
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				add_trait = just
				chance = 35
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_dishonored_maiden_compromise }
	}
	option = { #Give her a place at my court
		name = VIETmisc.8210.d
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				trait = kind
				trait = charitable
				trait = trusting
				trait = lustful
			}
			NOT = { trait = paranoid }
			NOT = { trait = proud }
			NOT = { trait = cruel }
		}
		prestige = -20
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = cruel
			}
			remove_trait = cruel
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				add_trait = kind
				chance = 45
			}
		}
		random = {
			add_trait = charitable
			chance = 35
		}
			
		create_character = {
			age = 16
			dynasty = random
			religion = ROOT
			culture = ROOT
			female = yes
			health = 5
			random_traits = no
			historical = yes
		}
		new_character = {
			#Education & other basic stuff
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_dishonored_deflowered_maiden
				duration = -1
			}
			#set_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_concubinage
			#set_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_marriage
			set_character_flag = no_court_invites
			add_trait = trusting					
			random = {
				VIET_give_clutter_artifact_effect = yes
				chance = 10
			}	
			#Flavor
			random_list = {
				85 = { } #Nothing
				15 = { add_scarred_tiered_effect = yes }
			}
			random_list = {
				40 = { } 
				30 = { add_trait = groomed }
				30 = { add_trait = fair }
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_loyal_servant
				who = ROOT
				years = 100
			}			
			if = {
				limit = { has_dlc = "Way of Life" }
				random_list = {
					60 = { add_trait = socializer }
					10 = { add_trait = scholar }
					10 = { add_trait = seductress }
					20 = {}
				}
			}
			#Personality Archetypes
			random_list = {
				20 = { # Innocent
					set_character_flag = VIET_dishonored_innocent
					add_trait = naive_appeaser
					add_trait = kind
					add_trait = patient
					add_trait = humble
				}
				20 = { # Nerd
					set_character_flag = VIET_dishonored_nerd
					add_trait = scholarly_theologian
					add_trait = erudite
					add_trait = diligent
					add_trait = slothful
					if = {
						limit = { has_dlc = "Way of Life" }
						random_list = {
							60 = { add_trait = scholar }
							10 = { add_trait = gamer }
							10 = { add_trait = mystic }
							10 = { add_trait = theologian }
							10 = {}
						}
					}
				}
				20 = { # Arrogant snob
					set_character_flag = VIET_dishonored_snob
					add_trait = thrifty_clerk
					add_trait = proud
					add_trait = stubborn
					add_trait = slothful
					if = {
						limit = { has_dlc = "Way of Life" }
						random_list = {
							60 = { add_trait = socializer }
							20 = { add_trait = schemer }
							20 = {}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_dishonored_maiden_help }
	}
}


# Vasha from Skyrim - capture notorious bandit wanted for murder, theft, and rape
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8211
	desc = VIETmisc.8211.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_judged_by_ruler
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	
	trigger = {
		#in_command = no
		#is_virgin_trigger = yes
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
		NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_vasha_was_here }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1	
				
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = craven
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = VIET_vasha_was_here 
	}

	option = { #Execute!
		name = VIETmisc.8211.a
		prestige = 20
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = arbitrary
			}
			remove_trait = arbitrary
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				add_trait = just
				chance = 50
			}
		}
		
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_captured_notorious_bandit
			duration = 1666
		}
	}
	option = { #Recruit him
		name = VIETmisc.8211.b
		prestige = -50
		wealth = -50
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = just
			}
			remove_trait = just
		}
		
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_hired_notorious_bandit
			duration = 1666
		}
		
		create_random_soldier = {
			#age = 16
			dynasty = random
			religion = ROOT
			culture = ROOT
			female = no
			health = 5
			random_traits = no
			historical = yes
		}
		new_character = {
			#Education & other basic stuff
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_notorious_bandit
				duration = -1
			}
			#set_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_concubinage
			#set_character_flag = ai_flag_refuse_marriage
			#set_character_flag = no_court_invites					
			random = {
				VIET_give_generic_weapon_effect = yes
				chance = 20
			}	
			#Flavor
			random_list = {
				250 = { } #Nothing
				100 = { add_scarred_tiered_effect = yes }
				20 = { 
					trigger = { has_dlc = Reapers }
					add_trait = one_eyed
				}
				20 = { 
					trigger = { has_dlc = Reapers }
					add_trait = one_handed
				}
				20 = { 
					trigger = { has_dlc = Reapers }
					add_trait = one_legged
				}
				5 = { 
					trigger = { has_dlc = Reapers }
					add_trait = one_legged
					add_trait = one_handed
				}
				5 = { 
					trigger = { has_dlc = Reapers }
					add_trait = one_legged
					add_trait = one_eyed
				}
				5 = { 
					trigger = { has_dlc = Reapers }
					add_trait = one_eyed
					add_trait = one_handed
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				40 = { } 
				20 = { add_trait = robust }
				20 = { add_trait = sturdy }
				20 = { add_trait = strong }
			}
			random_list = {
				60 = { add_trait = shrewd }
				20 = { add_trait = quick }
				20 = { add_trait = genius }
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_loyal_servant
				who = ROOT
				years = 100
			}			
			#if = {
			#	limit = { has_dlc = "Way of Life" }
			#	random_list = {
			#		10 = { add_trait = seducer }
			#		10 = { add_trait = duelist }
			#		10 = { add_trait = impaler }
			#		10 = { add_trait = schemer }
			#		10 = { add_trait = strategist }
			#		20 = {}
			#	}
			#}
			#Personality Archetypes
			add_trait = cruel
			add_trait = lustful
			add_trait = brave
			random_list = {
				20 = { # Suave and cunning gentleman
					set_character_flag = VIET_vasha_suave
					change_diplomacy = 3
					change_intrigue = 2
					add_trait = gregarious
					add_trait = erudite
					add_trait = proud
					add_trait = fair
					add_trait = scholar
				}
				20 = { # Rowdy fun-lover
					set_character_flag = VIET_vasha_partier
					add_trait = arbitrary
					add_trait = gluttonous
					add_trait = envious
					add_trait = hedonist
				}
				20 = { # Inhumane and immoral
					set_character_flag = VIET_vasha_asshole
					change_diplomacy = -5
					change_martial = 3
					add_trait = impaler
					add_trait = greedy
					add_trait = arbitrary
					add_trait = wroth
				}
				20 = { # All business
					set_character_flag = VIET_vasha_smuggler
					change_stewardship = 3
					add_trait = administrator
					add_trait = greedy
					add_trait = cynical
					add_trait = patient
				}
			}
		}
		
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_hire_vasha_choice }
	}
}


# Courtier boasts about supposed conquests of virgins
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8212
	desc = VIETmisc.8212.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_maiden
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		#is_virgin_trigger = yes
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
		any_courtier = {
			is_adult = yes
			is_female = no
			is_virgin_trigger = no
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			OR = {
				trait = lustful
				trait = proud
				trait = hedonist
				trait = seducer
				trait = gregarious
			}			
			is_married = no
			has_lover = no
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1	
				
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = diligent
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_adult = yes
				is_female = no
				is_virgin_trigger = no
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				OR = {
					trait = lustful
					trait = proud
					trait = hedonist
					trait = seducer
					trait = gregarious
				}			
				is_married = no
				has_lover = no
			}
			save_event_target_as = target_VIET_claiming_to_be_womanizer
		}
	}

	option = { #Punished in the afterlife!
		name = VIETmisc.8212.a
		trigger = {
			trait = zealous
		}
		tooltip_info = zealous
		piety = 5
		event_target:target_VIET_claiming_to_be_womanizer = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_defiler_of_maidens
				duration = 1519
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_publically_chastised_me
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_shameless_rake
				who = ROOT
				years = 3
			}
		}		
	}

	option = { #Amateur
		name = VIETmisc.8212.b
		trigger = {
			trait = seducer
			is_female = no
			NOT = { trait = homosexual }
		}
		tooltip_info = seducer
		prestige = 5
		event_target:target_VIET_claiming_to_be_womanizer = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_defiler_of_maidens
				duration = 1519
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_condenscending_attitude
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
			#reverse_opinion = {
			#	modifier = VIET_opinion_shameless_rake
			#	who = ROOT
			#	years = 3
			#}
		}		
	}

	option = { #Agree
		name = VIETmisc.8212.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					is_female = no
					NOT = { trait = homosexual }				
				}
				AND = {
					is_female = yes
					trait = homosexual
				}
			}
			is_virgin_trigger = no
		}
		#tooltip_info = seducer
		event_target:target_VIET_claiming_to_be_womanizer = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_defiler_of_maidens
				duration = 1519
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = agrees_with_me
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
			#reverse_opinion = {
			#	modifier = VIET_opinion_shameless_rake
			#	who = ROOT
			#	years = 3
			#}
		}		
	}

	option = { #Don't believe him
		name = VIETmisc.8212.d
		#trigger = {
		#	OR = {
		#		AND = {
		#			is_female = no
		#			NOT = { trait = homosexual }				
		#		}
		#		AND = {
		#			is_female = yes
		#			trait = homosexual
		#		}
		#	}
		#	is_virgin_trigger = no
		#}
		#tooltip_info = seducer
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = highly_amused_ruler
			duration = 365
		}
		event_target:target_VIET_claiming_to_be_womanizer = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_defiler_of_maidens
				duration = 1519
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_opinion_condenscending_attitude
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
			#reverse_opinion = {
			#	modifier = VIET_opinion_shameless_rake
			#	who = ROOT
			#	years = 3
			#}
		}		
	}

	option = { #Despicable attitude
		name = VIETmisc.8212.e
		#trigger = {
		#	OR = {
		#		AND = {
		#			is_female = no
		#			NOT = { trait = homosexual }				
		#		}
		#		AND = {
		#			is_female = yes
		#			trait = homosexual
		#		}
		#	}
		#	is_virgin_trigger = no
		#}
		#tooltip_info = seducer

		}

# Courtier is lacking in sexual experience
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8213
	desc = VIETmisc.8213.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_brothel
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		#is_virgin_trigger = yes
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
		any_courtier = {
			is_adult = yes
			is_female = no
			is_virgin_trigger = yes
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			NOT = { trait = celibate }
			NOT = { trait = eunuch }
			NOT = { trait = homosexual }
			#No close relatives unless incest is okay
			#NOT = { is_consort = ROOT }
			#NOT = { is_close_relative = ROOT }
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1	
				
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = diligent
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_adult = yes
				is_female = no
				is_virgin_trigger = yes
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				NOT = { trait = celibate }
				NOT = { trait = eunuch }
				NOT = { trait = homosexual }
				#No close relatives unless incest is okay
				#NOT = { is_consort = ROOT }
				#NOT = { is_close_relative = ROOT }
			}
			save_event_target_as = target_VIET_inexperienced_man
		}
	}

	option = { #What a loser
		name = VIETmisc.8213.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = kind
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = kind
				chance = 50
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = chaste
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = chaste
				chance = 25
			}
		}
		prestige = 5
		event_target:target_VIET_inexperienced_man = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_not_enough_sex_rumors
				duration = 730
			}
			random = {
				add_trait = depressed
				chance = 50
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_shamed_me
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
		}		
	}

	option = { #Go to the whorehouse
		name = VIETmisc.8213.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = chaste
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = chaste
				chance = 50
			}
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = advice_giver
			duration = 365
		}
		random_list = {
			50 = { #Accepts advice
				event_target:target_VIET_inexperienced_man = {
					add_trait = lustful
					wealth = -10
					prestige = 10
					opinion = {
						modifier = VIET_opinion_reasonable_advice
						who = ROOT
						years = 1
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_virgin_accepts_advice }
			}
			50 = { #Doesn't accept advice
				event_target:target_VIET_inexperienced_man = {
					add_character_modifier = {
						name = VIET_not_enough_sex_rumors
						duration = 730
					}
					random = {
						add_trait = depressed
						chance = 50
					}
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_shamed_me
						who = ROOT
						years = 1
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_virgin_rejects_advice }			
			}
		}		
	}

	option = { #Don't worry about others
		name = VIETmisc.8213.c
		random_list = {
			60 = {}
			20 = { add_trait = kind }
			10 = { add_trait = patient }
			10 = { add_trait = humble }
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = advice_giver
			duration = 365
		}
		event_target:target_VIET_inexperienced_man = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_not_enough_sex_rumors
				duration = 730
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_comforted_me
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
			random = {
				add_friend = ROOT
				chance = 33
			}
		}		
	}

	option = { # Teach a thing or two - male option
		name = VIETmisc.8213.d
		trigger = {
			is_female = no
			is_virgin_trigger = no
			NOT = { trait = eunuch }
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = advice_giver
			duration = 365
		}
		event_target:target_VIET_inexperienced_man = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_helped_me
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
			random = {
				add_friend = ROOT
				chance = 33
			}
			random = {
				add_trait = lustful
				chance = 20
			}
		}	
	}

	option = { # Teach a thing or two - female option
		name = VIETmisc.8213.e
		trigger = {
			is_female = yes
			NOT = { trait = homosexual }
			is_virgin_trigger = no
			is_unattractive_trigger = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				trait = zealous
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.05
				has_lover = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.05
				is_married = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				event_target:target_VIET_inexperienced_man = {
					is_unattractive_trigger = yes
				}
			}
		}
		event_target:target_VIET_inexperienced_man = {
			add_lover = ROOT
			random = {
				add_trait = lustful
				chance = 20
			}
		}		
	}
}

# Someone doesn't like broccoli
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8215
	desc = VIETmisc.8215.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_feast_hf
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	
	trigger = {
		#in_command = no
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
		OR = {
			culture_group = latin
			culture_group = iberian
			culture_group = byzantine
			capital_scope = {
				OR = {
					region = world_europe_south
					region = world_europe_south_east
					region = world_africa_north
					region = world_asia_minor
					culture_group = latin
					culture_group = iberian
					culture_group = byzantine
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1	
				
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {

			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {

		}
		modifier = {

			trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = diligent
		}
	}

	option = { # I like it
		name = VIETmisc.8215.a
		prestige = 3
	}
	option = { # Who am I to judge?

# Broccoli vs cauliflower
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8216
	desc = VIETmisc.8216.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
		OR = {
			culture_group = latin
			culture_group = iberian
			culture_group = byzantine
			capital_scope = {
				OR = {
					region = world_europe_south
					region = world_europe_south_east
					region = world_africa_north
					region = world_asia_minor
					culture_group = latin
					culture_group = iberian
					culture_group = byzantine
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1	
				
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = wroth
		}
	}

	option = { # Broccoli
		name = VIETmisc.8216.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = eating_good_food
			duration = 180
		}
	}
	option = { # Cauliflower
		name = VIETmisc.8216.b
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = eating_good_food
			duration = 180
		}
	}
	option = { # Ignore and move on
		name = VIETmisc.8216.c
		random_list = {
			70 = { }
			10 = { add_trait = humble }
			10 = { add_trait = shy }
			10 = { add_trait = slothful }
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = eating_good_food
			duration = 180
		}
	}
	option = { # Both!
		name = VIETmisc.8216.d
		random = {
			add_trait = gluttonous
			chance = 25
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = eating_good_food
			duration = 180
		}
	}
}
