# Dream of a great ship in a harbor
long_character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8217
	desc = VIETmisc.8217.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_columbus
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1	
				
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = craven
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = proud
		}
	}

	option = { # Ok
		name = VIETmisc.8217.a
		prestige = 1
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = craven
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = craven
				chance = 40
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				add_trait = brave
				chance = 30
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = shy
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = shy
				chance = 30
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				add_trait = gregarious
				chance = 20
			}
		}
	}
}

		days = 1

		}

			factor = 1.2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = proud
		}
	}

	option = { # A friend
		name = VIETmisc.8218.a

				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				is_adult = yes
				in_command = no
				is_abroad = no
				ai = yes
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				character_event = { id = VIETmisc.8219 } #ping
			}
		}
	}
}

# Meet someone you know irl in a dream
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8220
	desc = VIETmisc.8220.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_small_town
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # What a coincidence! Good reaction
		name = VIETmisc.8220.a
		FROM = {
			random = {
				add_friend = ROOT
				chance = 30
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_shared_dream_good
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_shared_dream_good
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # What a coincidence! Bad reaction
		name = VIETmisc.8220.b
		FROM = {
			random = {
				add_rival = ROOT
				chance = 15
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_shared_dream_bad
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = VIET_shared_dream_bad
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
		}
	}
}


# Dream of a Korean Drama (probably should've been considered an event chain but oh well)
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8221
	desc = VIETmisc.8221.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_modern_slice_of_life
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	
	trigger = {
		#in_command = no
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
		#Might be immersion breaking for some 
		NOT = {
			has_game_rule = {
				name = VIET_events_rules
				value = serious
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_generic_kdrama_happened_to_me }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1	
				
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = cruel
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = lustful
		}
	}

	option = { # Who am I?
		name = VIETmisc.8221.a
		set_character_flag = VIET_generic_kdrama_happened_to_me
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_kdrama_who_am_i }
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.3
						AND = {
							is_female = yes
							NOT = { trait = homosexual }
						}
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.3
						AND = {
							is_female = no
							trait = homosexual
						}
					}
					#set_character_flag = VIET_kdrama_girls_pov
					character_event = { id = VIETmisc.8222 } # girl's POV
				}
				50 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.3
						is_female = no
						NOT = { trait = homosexual }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.3
						is_female = yes
						trait = homosexual
					}
					#set_character_flag = VIET_kdrama_boys_pov
					character_event = { id = VIETmisc.8225 } # boy's POV
				}
			}		
		}
	}
}

# What is reality and what is dream?
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8231
	desc = VIETmisc.8231.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_recovery
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Reality
		name = VIETmisc.8231.a
		random = {
			add_trait = proud
			chance = 5
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_campfire_dream
			duration = 777
		}
	}
	option = { # Dream
		name = VIETmisc.8231.b
		random = {
			add_trait = lunatic
			chance = 5
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_campfire_dream
			duration = 777
		}
	}
	option = { # Cannot distinguish between the two
		name = VIETmisc.8231.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				learning = 11
				trait = erudite
				trait = scholar
				trait = theologian
				trait = lunatic
				religion = taoist #Zhuangzi
			}
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_navel_gazing
			duration = 777
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_campfire_dream
			duration = 777
		}
	}
	option = { # Dream within a dream
		name = VIETmisc.8231.d
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				learning = 11
				trait = erudite
				trait = scholar
				trait = theologian
				trait = lunatic
				religion = taoist #Zhuangzi
			}
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_navel_gazing
			duration = 777
		}

# Sunset dream with a companion
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8232
	desc = VIETmisc.8232.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_hyouka
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	#war = no
	
	#trigger = {
		#in_command = no
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
		#Might be immersion breaking for some 
		#NOT = {
		#	has_game_rule = {
		#		name = VIET_events_rules
		#		value = serious
		#	}
		#}
	#}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1	
				
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = shy
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.8232.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = shy
			}
			random = {
				remove_trait = shy
				chance = 25
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				add_trait = gregarious
				chance = 25
			}
		}
		piety = 2
	}
}

# Dream of a generic music-themed Kdrama titled "Music of Love"
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.8234
	desc = VIETmisc.8234.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_holy_light_basic
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	war = no
	
	trigger = {
		in_command = no
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = religion_names value = random } }
		#NOT = { has_alternate_start_parameter = { key = culture_names value = random } }
		#Might be immersion breaking for some 
		NOT = {
			has_game_rule = {
				name = VIET_events_rules
				value = serious
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_music_of_love_kdrama }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1	
				
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = poet
		}				
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = cruel
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = craven
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = slothful
		}
	}

	option = { # ok
		name = VIETmisc.8234.a
		set_character_flag = VIET_music_of_love_kdrama
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_music_of_love_kdrama_text }
		hidden_tooltip = {
			narrative_event = { id = VIETmisc.8235 }
		}
	}
}
